 When Sri Krishna killed King Narakasura of Pragjyotishpur (present-day Guwahati and adjoining area), he met Balarama in Mithila during his return to Dwarka and persuaded him to return
 kehete hai ki balram ke bahut saare saathi us pradesh main bas gaye! kya us ilaake main yadavon kii saghan aabaadi kaa us puranic ghatana se koi sambandh he? kya us ilaake kii bhashaa maithili or gujarati main kuch samanta hone kaa yah kaaran ho saktaa he? kya maithili, bangala, nepali or gujarati main kuch saamanta ke sutara us puranic ghatana main nihit ho sakate hai? yah gahan shodh kaa vishay he
 Although current historiography rejects folklore and folklore as evidence, scholars should also work in this direction
 saamaa chakeba or samb kaa mithila se sambandhth puja ke aasapaas hi mithila main saamaa-chakeba kaa lokparv manaaya jaataa he jo bhai-bahan ke atoot prem kaa pratik he
 Sama (or Shyama!) Was Krishna's daughter and Samb's sister
 saamaa par mantri churak (jise chugala kaha gaya) ne ek rishi se avaidh sambandh kaa aarope lagaaya jisapar krishna ne saamaa ko pakshi banane kaa shraap de diya
 Later Samb did penance and persuaded Krishna that he should curse Sama
 krishna ne kaha ki saamaa saal main ek baar aath dinon ke liye manushya rup main saamne aegi or usee dauraan saamaa-chakeba kaa parv manaaya jaataa he
 In folk songs, Minister Churak (chugla) is condemned and his mustache is set on fire
 gauratlab he ki saamaa-chakeba chhath ke kharnaa din shuru hota he or poornima din khatm
 sama-chakeba is celebrated in Mithila itself and says about the Chhath Vrat that prayers are given to remove incurable and serious diseases like leprosy, disability, scar, slander, disaster etc
 isse pehle ham varnan kar chuke hai ki samb ko kusht rog tha jiske liye shakaldeepi brahnmon ko shaq dweep se bulaayaa gaya tha or jo baad main magadh main based yaa phir se based! yahaan kuch na kuch aisa he jo samb, kusht rog, gujarat (dwarka), shakaldeepi brahman, surya-mandiron kii shrinkhalaa, chhath or saamaa-chakeba main ek maheen sambandh darshata he
 However, the question remains unanswered as to why the festival of sama-chakeba is celebrated only in Mithila, not in the areas of Gujarat or Braj! Are there signs of any such festival in the folk songs of Braj or Gujarat or other parts of the country? Probably these signs have not been found yet
 lekin sabase badi baat ye ki agar shakaldeepi brahmanon kii isamen bhoomika thi yaa unke prabhaav main parvarti raajaaon ne suryamandiron kaa nirmaan karaayaa to ek sawaal phir bhi anutarit he: chhath puja main mantron-karmkaandon or purohito kaa abhaav or samaaj ke har varg dwaara ise shraddha se manaaya janaa
 However one belief also relates to Buddhism
 surya, buddha or hindu paramparaon main bhi milte hai or kai saare surya mandir un raajaaon dwaara banawaye prathit hote hai jo buddha bhi the
 So was any method of Suryopasana developed that was priestly and ritual-less and which later took the form of Chhath? According to one legend, it is possible that Chhath Puja has been converted into a folk festival due to Karna of Anga-raj
 karn ko jeevanabhar soot-putra kaa laanchhan jhelana padaa tha or unhone surya se khud ko manyata dene kii prarthana kii thi aisa surya ne kiya bhi
 Karna's character is the character of a rebellion, and it is possible that later generations have turned that rebellion as a symbol, priestless and devoid of rituals
 chhath puja main vahi vasteen, fal yaa utpaada prayog main laae jate hai jo sthaneey hai
 But from that point of view, it seems that the beginning of Chhath Puja has started when human civilization was living only on fruits and flowers and did not learn to make sweets or the development of systematic farming
 samaaj main varna-vyavastha sthapit nahin hui thi yaa apane shuruaati rup main thi
 Overall, it can be said that Chhath festival is a great symbol of social harmony and generosity and perhaps the reason for its popularity here
 isamen agar ham pracheen mithila kii udaar janak-parampara or baad ke yug main kshetra kaa buddha dharm ke prabhaav main hona bhi jod den-to udaar paramparaon kii ek shrinkhalaa ban jaati he
 However, many perspectives are yet to come on Chhath festival

 ) vishwa vyapaar sarleekaran ke prati patibaddhta vyakt karte hue pradhanmantri narendra modi ne raashtrapati baraak obama ke saath baatcheet main aaj kaha ki vishwa vyapaar sanghathan (WTO) kii baatcheet main bharat kii khaadya suraksha sambandhi chintaaon kaa samaadhaan nikaala janaa chahie
 At the time of making a joint statement with Obama after the summit, Modi said, 'the WTO issue was discussed openly
 ham vyapaar sarleekaran kaa samarthan karte hai, par saath hi ham chaahate hai ki hamaari khaadya suraksha chintaaon kaa samaadhaan hona chahie or ham ummid karte hai ki aisa jald hi hoga
 It is noteworthy that India took a tough stand on the issue of food security at the WTO meeting in Geneva in July and refused to ratify the wto's Trade Facilitation Agreement (TFA)
 is samjhaute ko sweekaar karne ke liye viksit desh dabaav banaaye hue hai, haalanki khaadya suraksha ke uddeshy se bharat ke saarvajanik khadyann bhandaaran ke mudde kaa sthaayee samaadhaan kiye bina ve aisa dabaav bana rahe hai
 The farmers have been asked by the WTO to amend the modalities of calculation of agricultural subsidy in case of purchasing food grains at minimum support price and selling it to the poor at cheap prices
 WTO ke maujuuda niyamon main khaadya sabsidi ko khadyann utpaadan ke kul mulya kaa 10 fisadi par simit kiya gaya he
 Along with this, there is a provision to calculate the subsidy at the price of two decades ago
 bharat khaadya sabsidi kii gananaa ke liye khadyann mulya ke aadhaar varsh 1986-88 ko badalane kii maang kar rahaa he
 India wants the subsidy calculation to be changed in the base year keeping in mind various aspects, such as inflation and currency fluctuations
 aisi ashanka he ki jaise hi bharat apane khaadya suraksha kaarykram ko puri tarah lagu karegaa sabsidi kaa ankada WTO dwaara nirdhaarit 10 fisadi kii seemaa se adhik ho jayega
 If this happens, if a member country of the WTO complains against India, then India can be fined heavily
 modi ne kaha, 'WTO kii bali main hui mantristareey baithak main kaaphi khulkar charchaa ho chuki he, bharat vyapaar sarleekaran kaa samarthan karata he
 But, i hope we will be able to find a solution that will address our concerns on food security
 meraa maananaa he ki yah jald karnaa sambhav he

 modi ne kaha, 'raashtrapati or maine hamaari kai saajha aarthik praathamiktaaon par baat kii
 i am confident that India will achieve rapid economic growth and will see a lot of change
